ALIRAKYM ALISHER
20B030206
PROJECT

create table Customers (
    Customer_id bigserial not null primary key,
    fname varchar(100) not null ,
    lname varchar(100) not null ,
    city varchar(100) not null ,
    adress varchar(100) not null ,
    phonenum bigint not null ,
    email varchar(100) not null,
    Payment_id BIGINT REFERENCES Payment (Payment_id),
    UNIQUE (Payment_id)
);


create table Managers (
    Manager_id bigserial not null primary key,
    manager_fname varchar(100) not null ,
    manager_lname varchar(100) not null ,
    manager_phone bigint not null
);

create table Packages(
    Package_id bigserial not null primary key,
    Pack_type varchar(100) not null ,
    Pack_weight numeric(19,2) not null,
    Pack_adress varchar(100) not null,
    Pack_warning varchar(100),
    Pack_status varchar(100) not null,
    Pack_price money not null,
    Pack_time date,
    Location_id BIGINT REFERENCES Plane (Plane_id),
    Manager_id BIGINT REFERENCES managers (manager_id),
    customer_id BIGINT REFERENCES customers (customer_id),
    packdelivered_time date
);

create table Location(
    Location_id bigserial not null primary key,
    Current_location varchar(100),
    Plane_id BIGINT REFERENCES Plane (Plane_id),
    Truck_id BIGINT REFERENCES Truck (Truck_id),
    Warehouse_id BIGINT REFERENCES Warehouse (Warehouse_id)
);

create table Truck(
    Truck_id integer not null primary key ,
    state_name varchar(100),
    route varchar(100)

);

create table Plane(
    Plane_id integer not null primary key ,
    plane_name varchar(100),
    route varchar(100)

);

create table Warehouse(
    Warehouse_id integer not null primary key,
    Warehouse_adress varchar(100),
    Warehouse_phonenum varchar(100)
);

create table Payment(
    Payment_id BIGSERIAL NOT NULL PRIMARY KEY,
    Confrimation varchar(100),
    Subscription varchar(100)
);

DELETE FROM packages Manager_id ;
ALTER TABLE customers DROP package_id;
ALTER TABLE packages ADD manager_id BIGINT REFERENCES managers (manager_id);
ALTER TABLE packages ADD customer_id BIGINT REFERENCES customers (customer_id);
ALTER TABLE packages ADD Packdelivered_time DATE ;
ALTER TABLE packages DELETE UNIQUE(manager_id);
ALTER TABLE location ADD plane_id BIGINT REFERENCES plane (plane_id);
ALTER TABLE location ADD truck_id BIGINT REFERENCES truck (truck_id);
ALTER TABLE location ADD warehouse_id BIGINT REFERENCES warehouse (Warehouse_id);
ALTER TABLE location ADD UNIQUE(plane_id);
ALTER TABLE location ADD UNIQUE(truck_id);
ALTER TABLE location ADD UNIQUE(warehouse_id);
ALTER TABLE packages ADD location_id BIGINT REFERENCES location (location_id);
ALTER TABLE packages ADD UNIQUE(location_id);

SOLVED TASK

4.1
SELECT customer_id,fname,lname,package_id,confrimation,pack_time,truck_id FROM customers NATURAL JOIN packages NATURAL JOIN payment NATURAL JOIN location WHERE Pack_time > '2021-06-01' AND truck_id='1' AND confrimation='Confirmed';
4.2
SELECT customer_id,fname , COUNT(*) FROM packages NATURAL JOIN customers GROUP BY customer_id, fname;
SELECT MAX(customer_id) FROM packages;
4.3
SELECT customer_id,fname,lname,SUM(pack_price) FROM customers NATURAL JOIN packages GROUP BY customer_id,fname,lname;

4.3
SELECT pack_adress, COUNT(*) FROM packages GROUP BY pack_adress;

4.4
SELECT package_id FROM packages WHERE pack_status LIKE '%On the way%';

4.5
SELECT customer_id,fname, adress, SUM(pack_price) FROM packages NATURAL JOIN customers WHERE Pack_time > '2021-11-01' GROUP BY customer_id,fname,adress;
